\title{Class17}
\author{Alberto Carreno}
\date{3/4/2020}

\begin{document}
\maketitle

Here we analyze infection data for the 2019 novel Coronavirus COVID-19
(2019-nCoV) epidemic. The raw data is pulled from the Johns Hopkins
University Center for Systems Science and Engineering (JHU CCSE)
Coronavirus repository.

A CSV file is available here
\url{https://github.com/RamiKrispin/coronavirus-csv}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{url <-}\StringTok{ "https://tinyurl.com/COVID-2019"}
\NormalTok{virus <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{read.csv}\NormalTok{(url)}

\KeywordTok{tail}\NormalTok{(virus)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
##      Province.State Country.Region     Lat     Long       date cases      type
## 2772        Shaanxi Mainland China 35.1917 108.8701 2020-03-04     7 recovered
## 2773       Shandong Mainland China 36.3427 118.1498 2020-03-04     5 recovered
## 2774       Shanghai Mainland China 31.2020 121.4491 2020-03-04     4 recovered
## 2775        Sichuan Mainland China 30.6171 102.7103 2020-03-04    12 recovered
## 2776       Xinjiang Mainland China 41.1129  85.2401 2020-03-04     1 recovered
## 2777       Zhejiang Mainland China 29.1832 120.0934 2020-03-04    21 recovered
\end{verbatim}

\begin{quote}
Q1. How many total infected cases are there around the world?
\end{quote}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{total_cases <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{sum}\NormalTok{(virus}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{cases)}
\NormalTok{total_cases}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## [1] 149549
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\KeywordTok{table}\NormalTok{(virus}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{type)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## 
## confirmed     death recovered 
##      1520       203      1054
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\KeywordTok{sum}\NormalTok{(virus}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{type }\OperatorTok{==}\StringTok{ "death"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## [1] 203
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{inds <-}\StringTok{  }\NormalTok{virus}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{type }\OperatorTok{==}\StringTok{ 'death'}
\NormalTok{death_cases <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{sum}\NormalTok{(virus[inds,}\StringTok{"cases"}\NormalTok{])}
\NormalTok{death_cases}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## [1] 3254
\end{verbatim}

\begin{quote}
Q2. how many deaths linked to infected cases have there been?
\end{quote}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{inds <-}\StringTok{  }\NormalTok{virus}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{type }\OperatorTok{==}\StringTok{ 'death'}
\NormalTok{death_cases <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{sum}\NormalTok{(virus[inds,}\StringTok{"cases"}\NormalTok{])}
\NormalTok{death_cases}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## [1] 3254
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\KeywordTok{round}\NormalTok{(death_cases}\OperatorTok{/}\NormalTok{total_cases}\OperatorTok{*}\DecValTok{100}\NormalTok{,}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## [1] 2.18
\end{verbatim}

\begin{quote}
Q3. What is the overall death rate?
\end{quote}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\KeywordTok{round}\NormalTok{(death_cases}\OperatorTok{/}\NormalTok{total_cases}\OperatorTok{*}\DecValTok{100}\NormalTok{,}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## [1] 2.18
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{virus[,]}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}

\begin{quote}
Q4. What is the death rate in ``Mainland China''?
\end{quote}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{mainland_total_cases <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{sum}\NormalTok{(mainland}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{cases)}
\NormalTok{mainland_total_cases}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## [1] 133207
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{mainland_inds <-}\StringTok{  }\NormalTok{mainland}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{type }\OperatorTok{==}\StringTok{ 'death'}
\NormalTok{mainland_death_cases <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{sum}\NormalTok{(mainland[mainland_inds,}\StringTok{"cases"}\NormalTok{])}
\NormalTok{mainland_death_cases}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## [1] 2981
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\KeywordTok{round}\NormalTok{(mainland_death_cases}\OperatorTok{/}\NormalTok{mainland_total_cases,}\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## [1] 0.0224
\end{verbatim}

\NormalTok{Iran_inds <-}\StringTok{  }\NormalTok{Iran}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{type }\OperatorTok{==}\StringTok{ 'death'}
